rigs lam smra la zab yangs spobs pa'i sgo / /
thogs med 'byed byed rigs pa'i gzhung kun las / /
bsdus te grwa ru bkod pa'i par 'di yang / /
dpal ~X gyis mdzes shing rnam dpyod ldan ~X pas bskrun / /
dge tshogs chu khur mkha' dang mnyam pa las / /
dam chos gru char cher 'phel de las kyang / /
'gro khams dge bcu'i myu gu dar ba las / /
nges legs 'bras bzang myur du smin gyur cig /
blo gsal gzhon nu'i blo sgo yangs por bye / /
gzhung lugs rgya mtsho'i gzhung don kun rtogs nas / /
rgyal ba'i bstan la rgyal ba gnyis pa bzhin / /
rnam thar gtsang mas rnam mang 'gro 'dren shog /
'phrin las smin legs zur mda'i lcags kyu yis / /
snod bcud sred ldan legs tshogs kun drangs te / /
dus mtha'i lcags khams rdzogs ldan pa'i zla bar / /
nges par rin chen gsum gyis bsgyur du gsol / /
phan bde'i rtsa lag rgyal bstan dbyig gi mchog /
rigs lam 'phrul gyi brgal brtag byi dor gyis / /
skye dgu'i legs byas rgyal mtshan rtser mchod mthus / /
bkra shis bde legs char du bsnyil gyur cig / / /
